create table RM_1s(
    InstrumentID            CHAR(7),
    TradingDay              CHAR(8),
    UpdateTime              CHAR(8),
    OpenPrice               DOUBLE,
    HighestPrice            DOUBLE,
    LowestPrice             DOUBLE,
    ClosePrice              DOUBLE,
    Volume                  INT,
    PRIMARY KEY ( TradingDay,UpdateTime )
);
